CREATE TABLE `learn_user` (
  `uid` bigint(11) NOT NULL,
  `create_time` datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '´´½¨Ê±¼ä',
  `update_time` datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'ÐÞ¸ÄÊ±¼ä',
  `user_name` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'ÓÃ»§Ãû',
  `password` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'ÃÜÂë',
  `role` tinyint(2) NOT NULL COMMENT 'ÓÃ»§ÀàÐÍ',
  `phone` char(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `email` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `hand_portrait` mediumblob COMMENT 'ÓÃ»§Í·Ïñ',
  PRIMARY KEY (`uid`),
  UNIQUE KEY `pk_uid` (`uid`) USING BTREE,
  KEY `uq_user_name` (`user_name`) USING BTREE,
  KEY `fk_role_no` (`role`) USING BTREE,
  CONSTRAINT `role_no_fk` FOREIGN KEY (`role`) REFERENCES `role` (`rid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci;

CREATE TABLE `teacher` (
  `tid` bigint(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `create_time` datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '´´½¨Ê±¼ä',
  `update_time` datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'ÐÞ¸ÄÊ±¼ä',
  `gender` tinyint(4) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'ÐÔ±ð',
  `class_no` bigint(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '°àÖ÷ÈÎ£¨¿ÉÑ¡£©',
  `college_name` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'ËùÊôÔºÏµ',
  `teacher_no` char(8) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Ö°¹¤ºÅ',
  `user_no` bigint(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `teacher_name` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`tid`),
  UNIQUE KEY `pk_tid` (`tid`),
  UNIQUE KEY `uq_teacher_no` (`teacher_no`) USING BTREE,
  KEY `fk_t_user_no` (`user_no`),
  CONSTRAINT `fk_t_user_no` FOREIGN KEY (`user_no`) REFERENCES `learn_user` (`uid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=2139 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci;

CREATE TABLE `class` (
  `class_no` bigint(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `create_time` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `update_time` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `class_name` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `class_teacher` bigint(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `class_college_name` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`class_no`),
  KEY `fk_class_teacher` (`class_teacher`),
  CONSTRAINT `fk_class_teacher` FOREIGN KEY (`class_teacher`) REFERENCES `teacher` (`tid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=602313 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci;

CREATE TABLE `student` (
  `sid` bigint(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `create_time` datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '´´½¨Ê±¼ä',
  `update_time` datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'ÐÞ¸ÄÊ±¼ä',
  `gender` tinyint(4) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'ÐÔ±ð',
  `class_no` bigint(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '°à¼¶',
  `student_no` char(8) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Ñ§ºÅ',
  `user_no` bigint(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `student_name` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `email` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `phone` char(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`sid`),
  UNIQUE KEY `pk_sid` (`sid`),
  UNIQUE KEY `uq_student_no` (`student_no`),
  KEY `fk_user_no` (`user_no`),
  KEY `fk_class_no` (`class_no`),
  CONSTRAINT `fk_class_no` FOREIGN KEY (`class_no`) REFERENCES `class` (`class_no`),
  CONSTRAINT `fk_user_no` FOREIGN KEY (`user_no`) REFERENCES `learn_user` (`uid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=6 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci;

CREATE TABLE `course` (
  `cid` bigint(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `course_no` char(12) DEFAULT NULL,
  `course_name` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '¿Î³ÌÃû',
  `substitute_teacher` bigint(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'ÈÎ½ÌÀÏÊ¦',
  `update_time` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `create_time` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `start_time` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '¿Î³Ì¿ªÊ¼Ê±¼ä',
  `learn_time` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '¿ÎÊ±',
  `end_time` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '¿Î³Ì½áÊøÊ±¼ä',
  `course_type` tinyint(4) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '¿Î³ÌÀàÐÍ',
  `term` tinyint(2) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '¿Î³ÌÑ§ÆÚ',
  `academic_year` char(4) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '¿Î³ÌÑ§Äê',
  `course_desc` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '脡脧驴脦脢卤录盲脙猫脢枚',
  `course_place` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `course_max_count` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`cid`),
  UNIQUE KEY `pk_cid` (`cid`),
  UNIQUE KEY `uq_course_no` (`course_no`) USING BTREE,
  KEY `fk_substitute_teacher` (`substitute_teacher`),
  CONSTRAINT `fk_substitute_teacher` FOREIGN KEY (`substitute_teacher`) REFERENCES `teacher` (`tid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=14 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci;


CREATE TABLE `course_student` (
  `student_fk` bigint(11) NOT NULL,
  `course_fk` bigint(11) NOT NULL,
  `score` decimal(5,1) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '³É¼¨',
  `create_time` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `update_time` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `final_evaluation` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`student_fk`,`course_fk`),
  KEY `fk_course` (`course_fk`),
  CONSTRAINT `fk_course` FOREIGN KEY (`course_fk`) REFERENCES `course` (`cid`),
  CONSTRAINT `fk_student` FOREIGN KEY (`student_fk`) REFERENCES `student` (`sid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci;
CREATE TABLE `log` (
  `lid` bigint(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `url` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `log_type` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `log_method` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `params` longtext CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci,
  `session_token` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `client_ip` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `log_time` bigint(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `location` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `create_time` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`lid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=1192 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci;

CREATE TABLE `role` (
  `rid` tinyint(2) NOT NULL,
  `role_name` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '½ÇÉ«Ãû',
  PRIMARY KEY (`rid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci;

CREATE TABLE `permission` (
  `pid` int(2) NOT NULL,
  `permission_name` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`pid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci;

CREATE TABLE `role_permission` (
  `role_fk` tinyint(2) NOT NULL,
  `permission_fk` int(2) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`role_fk`,`permission_fk`),
  KEY `permission_fk` (`permission_fk`),
  CONSTRAINT `permission_fk` FOREIGN KEY (`permission_fk`) REFERENCES `permission` (`pid`),
  CONSTRAINT `role_fk` FOREIGN KEY (`role_fk`) REFERENCES `role` (`rid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci;
